msg:Children's Day is coming, let's check out the parent-child hotel that children are longing for

üõè „ÄêÔ∏èBeijing Crowne Plaza Airport Check-in Guide„Äë

üìå Hotel Overview

‚ù∂. Overall evaluation: If this is the best hotel in Shunyi District, it would be a bit exaggerated; but if you want to find another high-end hotel in Tianzhu Town (Tianzhu District) that can compete with the Airport CP and is not extravagant, there is really no rival. This kind of hotel hidden in the suburban villa area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe city is especially suitable for Beijing local "hotel control" to use for weekend "micro vacation" or "light vacation". Simply empty your mind, and then go to the Luo Hong Art Museum next door to eat and eat. Everything is graceful and woven by the heart. This is the real "small man wins everything".

üè® About the room In Room

‚ù∂. Room layout: Manager Sun of the front office depar**ent explained to us in detail the decoration style and layout of the 60-square-meter high-floor executive suite where we stayed this time, which was indeed professional. Honestly, the avant-garde and industrial style of brick-gray, the bump-proof rounded desk, the essential capsule coffee machine and other details are really much better than the old-fashioned binding of ochre red. I was attracted to it directly;
‚ù∑. Welcome gift: The welcome fruit plate has a rich variety of fruits, and the dragon fruit has been carefully trimmed and removed, making it more suitable for direct consumption; the richness of the welcome dessert is almost a replica and miniature version of Happy Hour, and the purple chocolate logo is solid.

‚òïÔ∏è Dining

‚ù∂. Gourmet glimpse: Breakfast is served from 6:30 to 10:00, and it will be delayed for half an hour on weekends or holidays, which is very humane. Manager Xia of the catering depar**ent always prepares freshly squeezed watermelon juice for my wife and children attentively and thoughtfully, and reserves the largest private room for us, which is warm and cozy. The old Beijing chef of the noodle stall is very talkative, and the authenticity of Lanzhou beef noodles is absolutely unambiguous; in addition, the old Beijing snacks (tofu brain/donkey rolls/pancakes...), Greek tomatoes, etc. are all worth trying; the executive lounge is on the 12th floor of Building 1. Rina (Xu Jiahui) always prepares my wife's favorite Baileys in advance. We forgot the items and took the initiative to return them to the room. Perhaps, the newly opened Pa County Edition‚Äôs housekeepers have such a service level, which is really a step-by-step enjoyment; ‚ù∑. City gluttony: Across the intersection is the European Plaza. The Fuquan Pavilion copper pot hot pot on the second floor is almost our family's canteen. It's delicious and not expensive. üèä Hardware Facilities Facilities ‚ù∂. Hotel environment: The hotel is divided into Building 1 and Building 2. The all-day restaurant and gym are in Building 1, and the newly renovated fashionable rooms are mainly in Building 2. Of course, the 3rd floor is connected by a sky corridor. If you are a resident of Building 1 and want to go to the gym, you don‚Äôt have to walk to the lobby. The design style of the atrium and public areas is very similar to that of InterContinental Hangzhou. In addition to the unparalleled sense of transparency, fashion, futuristic and fairy-tale, it also fits the heritage of an airport-type business hotel (the shape of a roc spreading its wings). By the way, the hotel has a free airport shuttle bus, and many domestic airline driver groups also choose this place as their first choice for overnight hotels. Therefore, among the six Beijing CPs we have stayed in, this one has the highest proportion of foreign guests - this also confirms the hotel's good reputation and high cost performance from the side;
‚ù∑. Swimming pool fitness: All the staff in the swimming pool are very doting on the two sons. Every time they go swimming, in addition to choosing the best resting position for us, they also provide the children with various functional drinks such as "Pocari Sweat" and "M Motion", which is very considerate.

üåü Unforgettable Moments
‚ù∂. Star employee: Vera, the guest relations manager, arranged everything for our family of four before, during and after our stay. Many times, we almost treated her as our own family. This kind of spontaneous intimacy cannot be faked. Only employees who really care about the guests will be able to feel their efforts most quickly. I have to give her a thumbs up;
‚ù∑. Number of stays: I have stayed in this hotel 16 times, and this is the 17th time. I am a little addicted to it, not because of the luxury of the hardware, but because the software and service are so warm and unforgettable (even the little boy who just joined the company and spoke tremblingly on the other end of the phone will make you feel the sincerity and truthfulness of his words. You will never want to get angry with such employees).

üìç Brief summary Conclusion

‚ù∂. Wonderful moments: There are 5 60-square-meter suites on each floor of the hotel. Our suite is in the middle, which is the best in terms of location and view. The hotel tennis court and the new National Exhibition Center are in full view. No wonder many famous automotive media bosses stay here every time the Beijing International Auto Show comes. When we stayed here at the beginning of last year, our family had just changed to a Zhiji L7 snake performance. At night, our two sons played with the ISC streamer and shadow smart light language in the hotel parking lot all night, which is still fresh in our memory. When we checked in today, my family‚Äôs 12th cat (the previous 11 cats have been given away) gave birth to five little cats, and Children‚Äôs Day is coming soon. It‚Äôs really a double happiness. See? Living in Crowne Plaza Linkong always has a good mood and good luck!
‚ù∑. Regrets: Most of the InterContinental hotels in China have standard management (of course, there are some exceptions like Yichang Yangtze River Express, where you give it good suggestions but it still makes all kinds of excuses for its mistakes. It is a hopeless hotel, haha). Even if regular guests nitpick, it is difficult to find major flaws. The same is true for this airport CP, which has almost no flaws and is worth staying in, especially in the off-season, when the price-performance ratio is very high (you know, during the Beijing Auto Show, this hotel is hard to find a room, and many executives of car companies stay here).
